<script>
function loadBoxMap() 
{
  var U=window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("http:", "https:"), QUEUE = [U, U.replace('leaflet', 'maplib'), U.replace('leaflet.js', 'boxMap.js?v=7.4')];
  
  if (typeof L  != 'undefined') QUEUE.shift(); //already loaded
    
  yepnope({load: QUEUE, complete: function()
  {
    window.waitMapsBmID = setInterval(function()
    {
      if (typeof L == 'undefined') return console.log('Leaflet not loaded yet[bm]...');
      if (typeof mL_createMap == 'undefined') return console.log('Maplib not loaded yet[bm]...');
	  if (typeof loadGMAP == 'undefined') return console.log('boxMAP not loaded yet[bm]...');

	  clearInterval(window.waitMapsBmID);

      window.mL_LoadMapJS = window.loadMapJS;
	  initBoxMapPopupOptions();
	  handleCallbackOSM(window.loadGMAP);
	}, 25);
  }});
}
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
function initBoxMapPopupOptions()
{  
if (typeof bAPI == 'undefined')
    window.bAPI = window; // for compatiblity with previous version
  var container = document.getElementById('bMAPpopUPpredefinedPAT');
  if (container !== null)
  {  
  
  }
  if (1 && typeof window.SKIP_OSM_EVENT_SHIELD == 'undefined' && typeof eventShield != 'undefined') 
{
  new eventShield('eventSHIELD', 'boxMAPborder', 1000);
  if (typeof document.getElementsByClassName != 'undefined')
  {
	  var md = document.getElementsByClassName('mapdiv');
	  if (md.length == 1)
	  {
		  md = md[0];
		  md.id = "mapdiv1234";
		  md.style.position = 'relative';
		  new eventShield('eventSHIELD2', md.id, 1000);
	  }
  }
}
}

if (typeof DrawColorPattern == 'function') initBoxMapPopupOptions();

</script>

					 <h2 class="featurette-heading" style="padding-bottom: 25px;">Our <span class="text-muted">Tools</span></h2>


					 <div class="col-md-6">
                       <h4><a href="http://www.city-data.com/city-compare/" title="">Compare two cities</a></h4>
                           <a href="http://www.city-data.com/city-compare/" title=""><img class="featurette-image img-responsive img-border lazy"   data-original="http://pics3.city-data.com/assets/desktop/section_tools/citycompare.jpg" alt="Compare two cities"></a>

                           <p>Use our city comparison tool to analyze and compare two cities. Geographical and statistical data, demographics, current and historical values - it’s all here. Making a decision on where to move is easier than ever!</p>
					 </div>
					 
					  <div class="col-md-6">
						<h4><a href="http://www.city-data.com/advanced/search.php" title="Advanced U.S. city search">Advanced U.S. city search</a></h4>
							<a href="http://www.city-data.com/advanced/search.php" title=""><img class="featurette-image img-responsive img-border lazy"   data-original="http://pics3.city-data.com/assets/desktop/section_tools/advsearch.jpg" alt="http://www.city-data.com/advanced/search.php"></a>
						<p>Find cities matching your requirements. Choose up to 10 criteria from our large database, set their desired ranges with easy-to-use visual controls and narrow the results using several available filters.
						</p>
					 </div>
					 
					 
				</div>

			    <div class="col-md-12 tools-window" style="margin-top: 25px;">

					  <div class="col-md-6">
						<h4><a href="http://www.city-data.com/MeetingPlace/" title="Ideal Meeting Place">Ideal Meeting Place</a></h4>
							<a href="http://www.city-data.com/MeetingPlace/" title=""><img class="featurette-image img-responsive img-border lazy"   data-original="http://pics3.city-data.com/assets/desktop/section_tools/meetingplace.jpg" alt="http://www.city-data.com/MeetingPlace/"></a>
						<p>This tool will help you find ideal meeting places between points, as well as the "travel radius" of a single point using different transportation modes. Unlike other tools that use simple approximations, the travel times in this tool are calculated using the road network analyzed with a routing algorithm.</p>
					 </div>


					 <div class="col-md-6">
						<h4><a href="http://www.city-data.com/travel-time/" title="">Travel Time Maps</a></h4>
                            <a href="http://www.city-data.com/travel-time/" title=""><img class="featurette-image img-responsive img-border lazy" data-original="http://pics3.city-data.com/assets/desktop/section_tools/travel.png" alt="Travel Time Maps"></a>

						<p>At City-Data, we gather location data for a wide variety of places. Using this data, we generate highly precise large-radius isochrone maps. We then utilize these isochrone maps to create user-friendly interactive maps that help you determine your travel time to the nearest location of your chosen category.</p>
					 </div>

										
			    </div>

					 <div class="col-md-12 tools-window" style="margin-top: 25px;">


					 <div class="col-md-6">


                                                <h4><a href="http://www.city-data.com/gas/" title="">Gasoline Usage Calculators for Trips</a></h4>
                                                <a href="http://www.city-data.com/gas/" title=""><img class="featurette-image img-responsive img-border lazy"   data-original="http://pics3.city-data.com/assets/desktop/section_tools/gasoline.jpg" alt="Gasoline Usage Calculators"></a>

                                                <p>
                                                Our Fuel Calculator allows you to determine the amount and cost of fuel for a trip, as well as compare both trip and yearly costs for two vehicles.             </p>


					 </div>
				</div>
			 </div>

									House and Property Values
								</a>
							</h2>
<p>We have collected assessment data for over 34 million properties around the United States. <div class="container space">
				<div class="col-md-7">
	            <h2 class="featurette-heading">What's on <span class="text-muted">City-Data.com</span></h2>
				<p>
					We have over 74,000 city photos not found anywhere else, graphs of the latest real estate prices and sales trends, recent home sales, a home value estimator, hundreds of thousands of maps, satellite photos, demographic data (race, income, ancestries, education, employment), geographic data, state profiles, crime data, registered sex offenders, cost of living, housing, religions, businesses, local news links based on our exclusive technology, birthplaces of famous people, political contributions, city government finances, employment, weather, natural disasters, hospitals, schools and libraries.
				</p>
<p>
In addition to our huge collection of data, we have also created our <a href="http://www.city-data.com/toplists.html">Top 100 City Lists</a> and <a href="http://www.city-data.com/top2/toplists2.html">Top 101 City Lists</a>. These lists rank cities in hundreds of categories, including income, crime, most gay couples, most cars, shortest commute, biggest houses, best educated residents and many more. We also have thousands of <a href="http://www.city-data.com/randomPics.php">random city pictures</a> submitted by our users.
</p>
	          </div>

        if ( pattern.test(elements[i].className) ) {

      }
    }
    return results;
  }

function menuRedesign()
{
var menu_more=$('#menu_dropdown');var menu_visible=$('#menu_visible');var menu_more_li=$('#menu_dropdown_li');var menu_container=$(".navbar-fixed-top > .container-menu");if($(".navbar-toggle").is(":visible")){menu_more.children().insertBefore(menu_more_li);menu_more_li.hide();}else{menu_more_li.show();var available_space=menu_container.width()-$(".navbar-header").outerWidth(true)-$("#search_bar_menu").outerWidth(true)-menu_more_li.outerWidth(true);var children=menu_visible.children();var curr_width=0;var reached_end=false;var i=0;var margin=8;for(;i<children.length;++i)
{var ch=$(children[i]);if(ch.prop("id")==menu_more_li.prop("id"))
{reached_end=true;break;}
if(ch.is(':visible'))
curr_width+=ch.outerWidth(true);if(curr_width+margin>available_space)
{break;}}
if(reached_end)
{var children=menu_more.children();for(i=0;i<children.length;++i)
{var ch=$(children[i]);ch.insertBefore(menu_more_li);if(ch.is(':visible'))
curr_width+=ch.outerWidth(true);if(curr_width+margin>available_space)
{ch.prependTo(menu_more);break;}}}else
{var topushfront=[];for(;i<children.length;++i)
{var ch=$(children[i]);if(ch.prop("id")==menu_more_li.prop("id"))
{break;}
topushfront.push(ch);}
for(i=0;i<topushfront.length;++i)
{var ch=$(topushfront[topushfront.length-1-i]);ch.prependTo(menu_more);}}}
menu_visible.removeClass("changing");menu_container.removeClass("changing");$(".navbar-collapse").removeClass("changing");
}

$(document).ready(function()
{
  menuRedesign();
  $(window).resize(function(){var menu_visible=$('#menu_visible');var menu_container=$(".navbar-fixed-top > .container-menu");menu_container.addClass("changing");menu_visible.addClass("changing");$(".navbar-collapse").addClass("changing");waitForFinalEvent(function(){menuRedesign();},100,'menu_auto_hide');});

	<script>
	

function handleScroll()
{  
  var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
  if (window.lastScrollTop === scrollTop) return;  
  window.lastScrollTop = scrollTop;
  
  if (scrollTop > 100)
    $('.scroll-top-wrapper').addClass('show');
  else
    $('.scroll-top-wrapper').removeClass('show');
}
   

function scrollToTop() {
    verticalOffset = typeof(verticalOffset) != 'undefined' ? verticalOffset : 0;
    element = $('body');
    offset = element.offset();
    offsetTop = offset.top;
    $('html, body').animate({scrollTop: offsetTop}, 500, 'linear');
}
   
$(document).ready(function()
{
  $('.scroll-top-wrapper').on('click', scrollToTop);
    
  var waiting = false, endScrollHandle = void 0;  
  $(document).on( 'ready', handleScroll); 
  $(document).scroll(function () 
  {
    if (waiting) return;
    waiting = true;

    // clear previous scheduled endScrollHandle
    clearTimeout(endScrollHandle);

    handleScroll();

    setTimeout(function () {waiting = false;}, 100);

    // schedule an extra execution of scroll() after 200ms in case the scrolling stops in next 100ms
    endScrollHandle = setTimeout(handleScroll, 200);
  });
    
});
 


	</script>

/* city autocomplete */
$(function(){
    function run(){
            function formatItemAutocomplete(row) {
                if(typeof(row[1]) != "undefined" && row[1] !== null) {
                    return row[0] + " (<i>pop. " + row[1] + "</i>)";
                }
            }

            $("#city_left").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })


            $("#city_right").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })
            $(".btn-submit").click(function () {
                $("#city_form").submit();
            });

            $('#city_left').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });
            $('#city_right').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });

    }
    run();
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {

        $(document.body).on('click', '#tab_dropdown li', function (event) {

            var $target = $(event.currentTarget);

            $target.closest('.btn-group')
                .find('[data-bind="label"]').text($target.text())
                .end()
                .children('.dropdown-toggle').dropdown('toggle');
            $('.tab-pane').each(function () {
                $(this).removeClass('active');
            });
            //ustaw aktywna klase
            $($target.find('a:first').attr('href')).addClass('active');
            //zmien ustawienia na ukrytych tabach
            $('.tabsol2 li').each(function () {
                if ($(this).find('a:first').text() == $('#dropdown-label').text()) {
                    $(this).addClass('active');
                } else {
                    $(this).removeClass('active');
                }
            });

            return false;

        });

        $(document).on('click.bs.tab.data-api', '[data-toggle="tab"]', function (e) {
            //przekopiowanie ustawienia tabow na selectbox
            $('.tab-pane').each(function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass('active')) {
                    $('#dropdown-label').text($(this).find('h4:first').text());
                }
            });
        })


        $('#myTab a').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault()
            $(this).tab('show')
        })

    });
	</script>


<script type="text/javascript">



$(document).ready(function() {

      //ustawienie selecta na city
      $('#dropdown-label').text($('#tab_dropdown').find('li:first').find('a:first').text());


      if ($(window).width() < 1200) {
          tabShortNames();
      }
      else
	  {
	  	    tabLongNames();
	  }

    $(window).resize(function() {
      waitForFinalEvent(function(){
        if ($(this).width() < 1200) {
            tabShortNames();
        } else {
            tabLongNames();
        }
      },200,'1');
    });




});

function tabShortNames() {
    $('.tab-list-short').each(function() {
        $(this).show();
    });
    $('.tab-list-long').each(function() {
        $(this).hide();
    });

    $('#map-tab-left').removeClass('col-md-5');
    $('#map-tab-right').removeClass('col-md-7');
    $('#map-tab-left').addClass('col-md-8');
    $('#map-tab-right').addClass('col-md-4');
}
function tabLongNames() {
    $('.tab-list-short').each(function() {
        $(this).hide();
    });
    $('.tab-list-long').each(function() {
        $(this).show();
    });

    $('#map-tab-left').removeClass('col-md-8');
    $('#map-tab-right').removeClass('col-md-4');
    $('#map-tab-left').addClass('col-md-5');
    $('#map-tab-right').addClass('col-md-7');
}

</script>


	<script>



	var searchBox=
	{
		delay: 400,
		hideTimeout: false,
		active: false,
		over: false,
		init:function(mob)
		{

			searchBox.check();
			$('#intelligent_search').mouseenter(function() {
				searchBox.over=true;
				searchBox.check();

			});

			$('#myCarousel').mouseleave(function() {
				searchBox.over=false;
				searchBox.check();
			});

			$('#intelligent_search').focus(function() {
				searchBox.active=true;
				searchBox.check();
			});

			$('#intelligent_search').blur(function() {
					searchBox.active=false;
					searchBox.check();
			});


			$('#intelligent_search').click(function() {
				searchBox.active=true;
				searchBox.check();
			});


		},
		check: function()
		 {
			 if(this.over || this.active)
			 {
				 if(this.hideTimeout)
				 {
					 window.clearTimeout(this.hideTimeout);
					 this.hideTimeout=false;
				 }
				// if(!$( "#search_bar_box" ).hasClass("search-active"))
				 window.setTimeout(function () {
				 $( "#search_bar_box" ).addClass("search-active");
				 $( "#search_bar_box" ).removeClass("search-inactive");
			 	},100);
			 }else
			 {
				 if(!this.hideTimeout)
				 {
	 				 this.hideTimeout = window.setTimeout(function () {
						 searchBox.hideTimeout=false;
	 					 $( "#search_bar_box" ).removeClass("search-active");
						 $( "#search_bar_box" ).addClass("search-inactive");
	 				},this.delay);
				}
			 }





		}



	};

	$(document).ready(function() {
	searchBox.init();
	$( "#search_bar_box" ).submit(function( event ) {
	 _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'homepage_searchbox', 'clicked','']);
	//  event.preventDefault();
	});
});

	</script>

 function ra(s,t){if (parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 2){document.write("<a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"",s,"\">",t,"</a>");}}function cdstats(){document.write('<if'+'rame width="1" scrolling="no" height="1" frameborder="0" allowtransparency="true" hspace="0" vspace="0" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" src="http://'+'www.city-data.com/'+'js/stats/tracker.html" name="cd_stats_frame"></iframe>');}

 function resizeFrame(f) {
 f.style.height = f.contentWindow.document.body.scrollHeight + "px";
 }
 function readCookie(name) {var nameEQ = name + "=";var ca = document.cookie.split(';');for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {var c = ca[i];while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);}return null;}
 function fpl_toggle(show){
 	// detect iphone
 	var agent=navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
 	var is_iphone = (agent.indexOf('iphone')!=-1);
 	c = readCookie('sflv');
 	if (show==1 && c=='hide') show = 0;
 	f = document.getElementById("lfp_container");
 	if (f){
 		if (is_iphone) {
 			f.innerHTML = '';
 			return false;
 		}
 		if (show){
                f.innerHTML = '<div id="lfp_ctrls"><span><a href="http://www.city-data.com/forum/">See the whole Forum</a> | <a href="#" onclick="fpl_toggle(0);return false;">Hide Forum Preview <img src="http://pics3.city-data.com/images/close.png" alt="Hide" /></a></span></div>'
                            + '<iframe name="lfp_frame" id="lfp_frame" src="http://www.city-data.com/forum/liveforum.php?b=d" frameborder="0"></iframe>';
 			if (show==2){
 				document.cookie="sflv=show;path=/;expires=Mon, 05 Jan 2032 14:17:41 GMT";
 			}
 		} else {
 			f.innerHTML = '<div id="lfp_showlink"><a href="#" onclick="fpl_toggle(2);return false;">Show Live Forum Preview</a></div>';
 			document.cookie="sflv=hide;path=/;expires=Mon, 05 Jan 2032 14:17:41 GMT";
 		}
 	}
 	return false;
     }

 


        function initCarousel(car) {
            $(car).find("img").each(function () { $(this).attr('src', $(this).data('src')); });
        }

        function loadTT() {
            var tt = document.createElement('script');
            tt.type = 'text/javascript';
            tt.async = true;
            tt.src = 'https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js';
            (document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0] || document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0]).appendChild(tt);
        }

        $(document).ready(function () {

            window.carIT = setInterval(function () {
                if ($.fn.carousel == void 0) return; //bootstrap js still not loaded
                clearInterval(window.carIT);
                $.fn.carousel.Constructor.TRANSITION_DURATION = 4000;
                $("#myCarousel").carousel({ interval: 9000 });
            }, 50);

		//lazyloading:
                    $('#mapOSM').lazyload({ appear: loadBoxMap });
        
            if ($(window).width() > 767) $('#lfp_container').lazyload({ appear: function () { fpl_toggle(1); } });



            $('img.lazy').lazyload({ threshold: 200 });
            $('#assessmentsCarousel,#restaurantsCarousel,#bottomCarousel').lazyload({ threshold: 200, appear: function () { initCarousel(this); }});
            $('#footer').lazyload({appear:loadTT});

        });

<p>除了能够看到灵魂，别无是处的普通高中生——黑崎一护有一天邂逅了一名少女，接着人生就发生了很大的转变。自称为死神的少女——朽木路奇亚，追着被称做虚的恶灵突然出现到了一护面前。由于一护的灵力很高，他就成为了虚下手的对像。身受重伤的路基亚无法解决恶灵，不得已只有把死神的能力分给一护，成为死神的一护与失去死神力量的路奇亚就一起开始了新的战斗……</p>                   </dd>                                    <dd class="info">                                        <span><span class='new'>完结：</span> <a href="/m427789/" target="_blank" title="第396话                               <p>是一部很不错的作品,世界观很像猎人早期的时候,很庞大的剧情结构...完全不像其名字一样...不会让人认为这是一部美食漫画...超越了"美食漫画"那渺小的格局...让我发现...哇!...原来美食漫画也可以这样画!...很JUMP的风格!...很有前景的美食漫画!...
本作是一部以“美食”为主的漫画作品，全身的肉在舌间融化并且浮出一层油的的野兽，一整年都结有美味虾蟹肉的树、流出源源不绝的香醇白兰地涌泉的泉水，这是一个探求未知的美味时代，每个美食家的人生菜单分为前菜、汤、鱼、肉、主菜、沙拉、甜点、饮料全8 种，美食四天王之一的特瑞科为了完成自己的全餐菜单，踏上了寻找珍奇美食的旅程。</p>                               </dd>                                    <dd class="info">                                        <span><span class='new'>完结：</span> <a href="/m757489/" target="_blank" class="mh-star-line star-4"></span>                                    </dd>                                    <dd class="label">                                        <a                              <p>JoJo奇妙冒险漫画 ，JOJO奇妙冒险漫画又称作JOJO奇妙历险记漫画，一曲歌颂人类的赞歌 19世纪末的一个雨夜，英国贵族祖斯达从昏迷中醒来，误将正在偷窃其财物的达利欧·布朗度当成了救命恩人。12年后，为了报恩祖斯达收养了布朗度的儿子迪奥，并且将其和自己的儿子祖纳桑一起抚养长大。但迪奥野心勃勃，成年后他不思报恩反而处心积虑的密谋夺取乔斯达家族的所有财富。不想东窗事发，穷凶极恶的迪奥逐丧心病狂杀害恩人祖斯达，并使用邪恶的石鬼面具里的魔力变成了一… 每一个人物，都被赋予了真正的灵魂……他们是独立的，拥有真正的人格，同时也就有了各种缺点，也许正因为这样，他们才一次次的，成功的占有了我的心……为他们感动，为他们担忧，为他们流泪……荒木先生为我们创造了一个怎样的世界啊！无论是善人还是恶人，还是平凡的人，他们的生命都在这里闪烁着光辉……</p>                                    </dd>
